// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/modelsmodels_mapobjects_console_under_generated.fx
// Shader: models/mapobjects/console/under
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/modelsmodels_mapobjects_console_rotate_generated.fx
// Shader: models/mapobjects/console/rotate
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	 float s_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.x;
	 float t_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.y;
	output.stage0.uv.x = s_stage0*cos(0.6981317 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * -sin(0.6981317 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(0.6981317 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(0.6981317 * gameTime));
	output.stage0.uv.y = s_stage0*sin(0.6981317 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * cos(0.6981317 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(0.6981317 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(0.6981317 * gameTime));

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_
	destination = (tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/modelsmodels_mapobjects_console_centercon_generated.fx
// Shader: models/mapobjects/console/centercon
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_scrolltext;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_scrolltext>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 0 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.y += -0.3 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	// Invalid or unparsed tcMod statement.
	 float s_stage1 = output.stage1.uv.x;
	 float t_stage1 = output.stage1.uv.y;
	output.stage1.uv.x = s_stage1*cos(0.6981317 * gameTime) + t_stage1 * -sin(0.6981317 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(0.6981317 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(0.6981317 * gameTime));
	output.stage1.uv.y = s_stage1*sin(0.6981317 * gameTime) + t_stage1 * cos(0.6981317 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(0.6981317 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(0.6981317 * gameTime));

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_scrolltext
	destination = (tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv)) + (destination);

	// stage1_
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/modelsmodels_mapobjects_console_console_generated.fx
// Shader: models/mapobjects/console/console
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_tinfx2c;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_console;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;
// stage2's externs
uniform texture stage2_console2;
uniform float3x2 stage2_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_tinfx2c>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_console>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage2_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage2_console2>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};
struct stage2_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD2;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
	stage2_input stage2;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_tinfx2c
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_console
	float4 stage1_source = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv);
	destination = (stage1_source * stage1_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage1_source.a));

	// stage2_console2
	destination = (tex2D(stage2_sampler, input.stage2.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	 float s_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.x;
	 float t_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.y;
	output.stage0.uv.x = s_stage0*cos(0.6981317 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * -sin(0.6981317 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(0.6981317 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(0.6981317 * gameTime));
	output.stage0.uv.y = s_stage0*sin(0.6981317 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * cos(0.6981317 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(0.6981317 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(0.6981317 * gameTime));
	output.stage0.uv.x += 5 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 0.4 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	 float s_stage1 = output.stage1.uv.x;
	 float t_stage1 = output.stage1.uv.y;
	output.stage1.uv.x = s_stage1*cos(0.6981317 * gameTime) + t_stage1 * -sin(0.6981317 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(0.6981317 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(0.6981317 * gameTime));
	output.stage1.uv.y = s_stage1*sin(0.6981317 * gameTime) + t_stage1 * cos(0.6981317 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(0.6981317 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(0.6981317 * gameTime));
	output.stage1.uv.x += 5 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv.y += 0.4 * gameTime;

	return output;
};

{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_spherex2
	destination = (tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv)) + (destination);

	// stage1_spherex
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

	stage1_input stage1;

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	 float s_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.x;
	 float t_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.y;
	output.stage0.uv.x = s_stage0*cos(17.43584 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * -sin(17.43584 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(17.43584 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(17.43584 * gameTime));
	output.stage0.uv.y = s_stage0*sin(17.43584 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * cos(17.43584 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(17.43584 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(17.43584 * gameTime));

// Shader: models/players/slash/yuriko
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_envmaproc;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_yuriko;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_envmaproc>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_yuriko>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_envmaproc
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_yuriko
	float4 stage1_source = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv);
	destination = (stage1_source * stage1_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage1_source.a));

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();

	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;

	float4 position : POSITION0;

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/modelsmodels_mapobjects_pipe_pipe02x_generated.fx
// Shader: models/mapobjects/pipe/pipe02x
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_tinfx2b;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_electricslime_old;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_tinfx2b>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_electricslime_old>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage0.uv.x *= 1;
	output.stage0.uv.y *= 0.5;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv.x += 7.2 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv.y += 1 * gameTime;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_tinfx2b
	destination = (tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv)) + (destination);

	// stage1_electricslime_old
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{

// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_monkeyhead;

// stage1's externs

{

	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_monkeyheadb>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{

	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;

	return destination;

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/modelsmodels_mapobjects_jets_jet_1_generated.fx
// Shader: models/mapobjects/jets/jet_1
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_jet_1;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_jet_2;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_jet_1>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_jet_2>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage0.uv.x *= 2;
	output.stage0.uv.y *= 1;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 6 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 0 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv.x += 3 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv.y += -0.5 * gameTime;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_jet_1
	destination = (tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv)) + (destination);

	// stage1_jet_2
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

// Shader: models/mapobjects/cross/cross
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_firewalla;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_cross;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_firewalla>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_cross>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage0.uv.x *= 0.25;
	output.stage0.uv.y *= 0.25;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 0.1 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 2 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_firewalla
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_cross
	float4 stage1_source = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv);
	destination = (stage1_source * stage1_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage1_source.a));

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/modelsmodels_mapobjects_banner_q3banner04_generated.fx
// Shader: models/mapobjects/banner/q3banner04
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_firegorre2;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_bolts;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;
// stage2's externs
uniform texture stage2_firegorre2;
uniform float3x2 stage2_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_firegorre2>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_bolts>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage2_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage2_firegorre2>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};
struct stage2_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD2;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
	stage2_input stage2;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage0.uv.x *= 20;
	output.stage0.uv.y *= 10;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 1 - sin(((((input.position.x + input.position.z) * 0.001 + (0.6 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.25;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 1 - sin(((((input.position.y) * 0.001 + (0.6 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.25;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 0.4 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 0.3 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv.x *= 5;
	output.stage1.uv.y *= 5;
	 float s_stage1 = output.stage1.uv.x;
	 float t_stage1 = output.stage1.uv.y;
	output.stage1.uv.x = s_stage1*cos(17.43584 * gameTime) + t_stage1 * -sin(17.43584 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(17.43584 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(17.43584 * gameTime));
	output.stage1.uv.y = s_stage1*sin(17.43584 * gameTime) + t_stage1 * cos(17.43584 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(17.43584 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(17.43584 * gameTime));
	output.stage1.uv.x += 9 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv.y += 9 * gameTime;
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage2.uv.x *= 0.2;
	output.stage2.uv.y *= 0.2;
	output.stage2.uv.x += 0.09 * gameTime;
	output.stage2.uv.y += 0.04 * gameTime;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_firegorre2
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_bolts
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv)) + (destination);

	// stage2_firegorre2
	destination = (tex2D(stage2_sampler, input.stage2.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;

// Shader: models/players/grunt/stripe_h
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_electricgrade3;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_stripe_h;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_electricgrade3>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_stripe_h>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 0 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.y += -0.5 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_electricgrade3
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_stripe_h
	float4 stage1_source = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv);
	destination = (stage1_source * stage1_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage1_source.a));

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

	stage1_input stage1;

// Shader: models/mapobjects/grenadel/grenadelx
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	 float s_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.x;
	 float t_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.y;
	output.stage0.uv.x = s_stage0*cos(0.1745329 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * -sin(0.1745329 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(0.1745329 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(0.1745329 * gameTime));
	output.stage0.uv.y = s_stage0*sin(0.1745329 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * cos(0.1745329 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(0.1745329 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(0.1745329 * gameTime));

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{

	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);

{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	 float s_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.x;
	 float t_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.y;
	output.stage0.uv.x = s_stage0*cos(5.811946 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * -sin(5.811946 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(5.811946 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(5.811946 * gameTime));
	output.stage0.uv.y = s_stage0*sin(5.811946 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * cos(5.811946 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(5.811946 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(5.811946 * gameTime));
	// Invalid or unparsed tcMod statement.

	 float s_stage1 = output.stage1.uv.x;
	 float t_stage1 = output.stage1.uv.y;
	output.stage1.uv.x = s_stage1*cos(-5.253441 * gameTime) + t_stage1 * -sin(-5.253441 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(-5.253441 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(-5.253441 * gameTime));
	output.stage1.uv.y = s_stage1*sin(-5.253441 * gameTime) + t_stage1 * cos(-5.253441 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(-5.253441 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(-5.253441 * gameTime));
	// Invalid or unparsed tcMod statement.

	return output;

	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;

{
	Texture = <stage2_xaero_h>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};
struct stage2_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD2;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
	stage2_input stage2;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv.x += 0.1 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv.y += 1 * gameTime;
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_xaero_h
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_firewalla
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv)) + (destination);

	// stage2_xaero_h
	float4 stage2_source = tex2D(stage2_sampler, input.stage2.uv);
	destination = (stage2_source * stage2_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage2_source.a));

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

	float3 normal : NORMAL0;

	stage1_input stage1;
	stage2_input stage2;

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)

	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv.x *= 0.5;
	output.stage1.uv.y *= 0.5;
	output.stage1.uv.x += 2 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv.y += 2 * gameTime;
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;

	destination = (stage2_source * stage2_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage2_source.a));

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

	float3 normal : NORMAL0;

	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	 float s_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.x;
	 float t_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.y;
	output.stage0.uv.x = s_stage0*cos(5.811946 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * -sin(5.811946 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(5.811946 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(5.811946 * gameTime));
	output.stage0.uv.y = s_stage0*sin(5.811946 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * cos(5.811946 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(5.811946 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(5.811946 * gameTime));
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	 float s_stage1 = output.stage1.uv.x;
	 float t_stage1 = output.stage1.uv.y;
	output.stage1.uv.x = s_stage1*cos(-1.745329 * gameTime) + t_stage1 * -sin(-1.745329 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(-1.745329 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(-1.745329 * gameTime));
	output.stage1.uv.y = s_stage1*sin(-1.745329 * gameTime) + t_stage1 * cos(-1.745329 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(-1.745329 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(-1.745329 * gameTime));

	return output;
};

	// stage1_
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
	stage2_input stage2;

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 1 - sin(((((input.position.x + input.position.z) * 0.001 + (0.7 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.5;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 1 - sin(((((input.position.y) * 0.001 + (0.7 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.5;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 1 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.y += -1 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.x *= 2;
	output.stage0.uv.y *= 2;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv.x *= 1.428571;
	output.stage1.uv.y *= 1.428571;
	output.stage1.uv.x += 1 - sin(((((input.position.x + input.position.z) * 0.001 + (0.3 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.4;
	output.stage1.uv.y += 1 - sin(((((input.position.y) * 0.001 + (0.3 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.4;
	output.stage1.uv.x += 0.7 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv.y += -0.4 * gameTime;
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;

	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_roderic>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 0 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 1 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 1 - sin(((((input.position.x + input.position.z) * 0.001 + (1.6 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.25;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 1 - sin(((((input.position.y) * 0.001 + (1.6 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.25;
	output.stage0.uv.x *= 0.25;
	output.stage0.uv.y *= 0.25;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_firegorre
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_roderic
	float4 stage1_source = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv);
	destination = (stage1_source * stage1_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage1_source.a));

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

{
	pass Pass1

		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}

	output.stage1.uv.y *= 2;
	output.stage1.uv.x += -1.7 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv.y += -0.3 * gameTime;
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage2.uv.x *= 1;
	output.stage2.uv.y *= 2;
	output.stage2.uv.x += -1.1 * gameTime;
	output.stage2.uv.y += -0.3 * gameTime;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_podiumfx1
	destination = (tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv)) + (destination);

	// stage1_podiumfx1b
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv)) + (destination);

	// stage2_podiumfx1b
	destination = (tex2D(stage2_sampler, input.stage2.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;

{
	Texture = <stage0_whiteimage>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_wrack>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};

	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{

	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_whiteimage
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_wrack
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv) * destination) + (destination * tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv).a);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/modelsmodels_players_visor_gorre_generated.fx
// Shader: models/players/visor/gorre
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_firegorre;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_gorre;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_firegorre>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_gorre>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 0 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 1 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 1 - sin(((((input.position.x + input.position.z) * 0.001 + (1.6 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.25;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 1 - sin(((((input.position.y) * 0.001 + (1.6 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.25;
	output.stage0.uv.x *= 0.25;
	output.stage0.uv.y *= 0.25;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_firegorre
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_gorre
	float4 stage1_source = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv);
	destination = (stage1_source * stage1_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage1_source.a));

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/modelsmodels_players_doom_phobos_generated.fx
// Shader: models/players/doom/phobos
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_phobos_fx;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_phobos;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_phobos_fx>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_phobos>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage0.uv.x *= 0.1428571;
	output.stage0.uv.y *= 0.1428571;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 5 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.y += -5 * gameTime;
	 float s_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.x;
	 float t_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.y;
	output.stage0.uv.x = s_stage0*cos(6.283185 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * -sin(6.283185 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(6.283185 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(6.283185 * gameTime));
	output.stage0.uv.y = s_stage0*sin(6.283185 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * cos(6.283185 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(6.283185 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(6.283185 * gameTime));
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_phobos_fx
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_phobos
	float4 stage1_source = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv);
	destination = (stage1_source * stage1_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage1_source.a));

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_proto_grueldark;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_torso;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_proto_grueldark>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_torso>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage0.uv.x *= 0.25;
	output.stage0.uv.y *= 0.25;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 0 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.y += -0.09 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 1 - sin(((((input.position.x + input.position.z) * 0.001 + (0.05 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.05;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 1 - sin(((((input.position.y) * 0.001 + (0.05 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.05;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_proto_grueldark
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_torso
	float4 stage1_source = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv);
	destination = (stage1_source * stage1_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage1_source.a));

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

// Shader: models/players/lucy/h_angel
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_h_angel;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_hologirl2;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_h_angel>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_hologirl2>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv.x += -6 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv.y += -0.2 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv.x *= 1;
	output.stage1.uv.y *= 1;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_h_angel
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_hologirl2
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/modelsmodels_mapobjects_lamps_bot_flare_generated.fx
// Shader: models/mapobjects/lamps/bot_flare
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	 float s_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.x;
	 float t_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.y;
	output.stage0.uv.x = s_stage0*cos(0.3490658 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * -sin(0.3490658 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(0.3490658 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(0.3490658 * gameTime));
	output.stage0.uv.y = s_stage0*sin(0.3490658 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * cos(0.3490658 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(0.3490658 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(0.3490658 * gameTime));

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_
	destination = (tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/modelsmodels_mapobjects_chain_chain3_generated.fx
// Shader: models/mapobjects/chain/chain3
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_whiteimage;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_chain3;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;
// stage2's externs
uniform texture stage2_chain3;
uniform float3x2 stage2_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_whiteimage>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_chain3>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage2_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage2_chain3>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};
struct stage2_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD2;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
	stage2_input stage2;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_whiteimage
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_chain3
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv) * destination) + (destination * tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv).a);

	// stage2_chain3
	destination = tex2D(stage2_sampler, input.stage2.uv) * destination;

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/modelsmodels_flags_r_flag2_generated.fx
// Shader: models/flags/r_flag2
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_r_flag2;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_red_fx;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;
// stage2's externs
uniform texture stage2_r_flag2;
uniform float3x2 stage2_tcmod;
// stage3's externs
uniform texture stage3_shadow;
uniform float3x2 stage3_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_r_flag2>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_red_fx>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage2_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage2_r_flag2>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage3_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage3_shadow>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};
struct stage2_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD2;
};
struct stage3_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD3;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
	stage2_input stage2;
	stage3_input stage3;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage3.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_r_flag2
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_red_fx
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv)) + (destination);

	// stage2_r_flag2
	float4 stage2_source = tex2D(stage2_sampler, input.stage2.uv);
	destination = (stage2_source * stage2_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage2_source.a));

	// stage3_shadow
	destination = tex2D(stage3_sampler, input.stage3.uv) * destination;

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}

// Generic Externs

sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_hologirl2>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input

{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;

};

{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv.x += -6 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv.y += -0.2 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv.x *= 1;
	output.stage1.uv.y *= 1;

	// stage1_hologirl2

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	 float s_stage1 = output.stage1.uv.x;
	 float t_stage1 = output.stage1.uv.y;
	output.stage1.uv.x = s_stage1*cos(7.033677 * gameTime) + t_stage1 * -sin(7.033677 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(7.033677 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(7.033677 * gameTime));
	output.stage1.uv.y = s_stage1*sin(7.033677 * gameTime) + t_stage1 * cos(7.033677 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(7.033677 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(7.033677 * gameTime));
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;
	 float s_stage2 = output.stage2.uv.x;
	 float t_stage2 = output.stage2.uv.y;
	output.stage2.uv.x = s_stage2*cos(-1.745329 * gameTime) + t_stage2 * -sin(-1.745329 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(-1.745329 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(-1.745329 * gameTime));
	output.stage2.uv.y = s_stage2*sin(-1.745329 * gameTime) + t_stage2 * cos(-1.745329 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(-1.745329 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(-1.745329 * gameTime));

	return output;

	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	 float s_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.x;
	 float t_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.y;
	output.stage0.uv.x = s_stage0*cos(6.108653 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * -sin(6.108653 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(6.108653 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(6.108653 * gameTime));
	output.stage0.uv.y = s_stage0*sin(6.108653 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * cos(6.108653 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(6.108653 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(6.108653 * gameTime));
	output.stage0.uv.x += 3 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 1 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0

// Shader: models/players/mynx/mynx_shiny
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_specular5;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs

{
	Texture = <stage0_specular5>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_mynx_shiny>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_specular5
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_mynx_shiny
	float4 stage1_source = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv);
	destination = (stage1_source * stage1_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage1_source.a));

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

// Shader: models/players/razor/patriot
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_whiteimage;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_patriot;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_whiteimage>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_patriot>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_whiteimage
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_patriot
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv) * destination) + (destination * tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv).a);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/modelsmodels_weapons2_lightning_trail_generated.fx
// Shader: models/weapons2/lightning/trail
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_trail;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_trail;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_trail>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_trail>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 3.1 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 1 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv.x += -1.7 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv.y += 1 * gameTime;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_trail
	destination = (tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv)) + (destination);

	// stage1_trail
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();

// Shader: models/players/orbb/orbb_h2
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_orbb_h2;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_tinfx;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;
// stage2's externs
uniform texture stage2_orbb_h2;
uniform float3x2 stage2_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_orbb_h2>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_tinfx>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage2_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage2_orbb_h2>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};
struct stage2_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD2;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
	stage2_input stage2;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_orbb_h2
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_tinfx
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv)) + (destination);

	// stage2_orbb_h2
	float4 stage2_source = tex2D(stage2_sampler, input.stage2.uv);
	destination = (stage2_source * stage2_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage2_source.a));

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

	}

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/modelsmodels_players_orbb_red_h_generated.fx
// Shader: models/players/orbb/red_h
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_red_h;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_red_h>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	 float s_stage1 = output.stage1.uv.x;
	 float t_stage1 = output.stage1.uv.y;
	output.stage1.uv.x = s_stage1*cos(1.570796 * gameTime) + t_stage1 * -sin(1.570796 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(1.570796 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(1.570796 * gameTime));
	output.stage1.uv.y = s_stage1*sin(1.570796 * gameTime) + t_stage1 * cos(1.570796 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(1.570796 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(1.570796 * gameTime));
	// Invalid or unparsed tcMod statement.

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_red_h
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_
	float4 stage1_source = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv);
	destination = (stage1_source * stage1_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage1_source.a));

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/modelsmodels_mapobjects_bitch_orb_generated.fx
// Shader: models/mapobjects/bitch/orb
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	 float s_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.x;
	 float t_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.y;
	output.stage0.uv.x = s_stage0*cos(0.5235988 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * -sin(0.5235988 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(0.5235988 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(0.5235988 * gameTime));
	output.stage0.uv.y = s_stage0*sin(0.5235988 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * cos(0.5235988 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(0.5235988 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(0.5235988 * gameTime));

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_
	destination = (tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/modelsmodels_mapobjects_bitch_forearm_generated.fx
// Shader: models/mapobjects/bitch/forearm
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_forearm;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_forearm01;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;
// stage2's externs
uniform texture stage2_forearm02;
uniform float3x2 stage2_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_forearm>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_forearm01>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage2_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage2_forearm02>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};
struct stage2_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD2;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
	stage2_input stage2;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv.x += 2.2 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv.y += 0 * gameTime;
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage2.uv.x += -1.1 * gameTime;
	output.stage2.uv.y += 0 * gameTime;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_forearm
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_forearm01
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv)) + (destination);

	// stage2_forearm02
	destination = (tex2D(stage2_sampler, input.stage2.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/modelsmodels_mapobjects_teleporter_energy_generated.fx
// Shader: models/mapobjects/teleporter/energy
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_energy;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_energy2;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;
// stage2's externs
uniform texture stage2_energy3;
uniform float3x2 stage2_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_energy>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_energy2>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage2_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage2_energy3>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};
struct stage2_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD2;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
	stage2_input stage2;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 2.2 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 1.3 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv.x += -1 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv.y += 0.5 * gameTime;
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage2.uv.x += 3 * gameTime;
	output.stage2.uv.y += 0 * gameTime;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_energy
	destination = (tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv)) + (destination);

	// stage1_energy2
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv)) + (destination);

	// stage2_energy3
	destination = (tex2D(stage2_sampler, input.stage2.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

// Shader: models/mapobjects/jesus/jesuswall
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_lightmap;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_jesuswall;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_lightmap>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_jesuswall>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.lightmapcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_lightmap
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_jesuswall
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv) * destination) + (destination * tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv).a);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_weed01
	float4 stage0_source = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);
	destination = (stage0_source * stage0_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage0_source.a));

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/modelsmodels_powerups_ammo_bfgammo_generated.fx
// Shader: models/powerups/ammo/bfgammo
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_envmapbfg;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_tinfx2;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;
// stage2's externs
uniform texture stage2_bfgammo;
uniform float3x2 stage2_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_envmapbfg>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_tinfx2>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage2_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage2_bfgammo>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};
struct stage2_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD2;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
	stage2_input stage2;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	 float s_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.x;
	 float t_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.y;
	output.stage0.uv.x = s_stage0*cos(6.108653 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * -sin(6.108653 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(6.108653 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(6.108653 * gameTime));
	output.stage0.uv.y = s_stage0*sin(6.108653 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * cos(6.108653 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(6.108653 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(6.108653 * gameTime));
	output.stage0.uv.x += 3 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 1 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_envmapbfg
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_tinfx2
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv)) + (destination);

	// stage2_bfgammo
	float4 stage2_source = tex2D(stage2_sampler, input.stage2.uv);
	destination = (stage2_source * stage2_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage2_source.a));

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

// Shader: models/powerups/ammo/grenammo
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_tinfx2d;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_grenammo;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_tinfx2d>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_grenammo>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_grenammo
	float4 stage1_source = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv);
	destination = (stage1_source * stage1_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage1_source.a));

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}
