// Shader: models/powerups/ammo/lighammo
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_envmapligh;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_lighammo;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_envmapligh>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_lighammo>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	 float s_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.x;
	 float t_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.y;
	output.stage0.uv.x = s_stage0*cos(6.108653 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * -sin(6.108653 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(6.108653 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(6.108653 * gameTime));
	output.stage0.uv.y = s_stage0*sin(6.108653 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * cos(6.108653 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(6.108653 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(6.108653 * gameTime));
	output.stage0.uv.x += 3 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 1 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_envmapligh
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_lighammo
	float4 stage1_source = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv);
	destination = (stage1_source * stage1_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage1_source.a));

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}

{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	 float s_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.x;
	 float t_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.y;
	output.stage0.uv.x = s_stage0*cos(6.108653 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * -sin(6.108653 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(6.108653 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(6.108653 * gameTime));
	output.stage0.uv.y = s_stage0*sin(6.108653 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * cos(6.108653 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(6.108653 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(6.108653 * gameTime));
	output.stage0.uv.x += 3 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 1 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_envmapplas
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_plasammo
	float4 stage1_source = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv);
	destination = (stage1_source * stage1_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage1_source.a));

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/modelsmodels_powerups_health_red_generated.fx
// Shader: models/powerups/health/red
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_envmapgold;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_kenelectric;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_envmapgold>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_kenelectric>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv.x *= 0.5;
	output.stage1.uv.y *= 0.5;
	 float s_stage1 = output.stage1.uv.x;
	 float t_stage1 = output.stage1.uv.y;
	output.stage1.uv.x = s_stage1*cos(5.811946 * gameTime) + t_stage1 * -sin(5.811946 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(5.811946 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(5.811946 * gameTime));
	output.stage1.uv.y = s_stage1*sin(5.811946 * gameTime) + t_stage1 * cos(5.811946 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(5.811946 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(5.811946 * gameTime));
	output.stage1.uv.x += 9 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv.y += 9 * gameTime;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_envmapgold
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_kenelectric
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	 float s_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.x;
	 float t_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.y;
	output.stage0.uv.x = s_stage0*cos(0.5235988 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * -sin(0.5235988 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(0.5235988 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(0.5235988 * gameTime));
	output.stage0.uv.y = s_stage0*sin(0.5235988 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * cos(0.5235988 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(0.5235988 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(0.5235988 * gameTime));
	output.stage0.uv.x += 1 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 1 * gameTime;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_envmaprail
	destination = (tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/modelsmodels_mapobjects_arenalogo_generated.fx
// Shader: models/mapobjects/arenalogo
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_quadmap;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_quadmap>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 1 - sin(((((input.position.x + input.position.z) * 0.001 + (0.2 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 1;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 1 - sin(((((input.position.y) * 0.001 + (0.2 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 1;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_quadmap
	destination = (tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}

	 float s_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.x;
	 float t_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.y;
	output.stage0.uv.x = s_stage0*cos(6.283185 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * -sin(6.283185 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(6.283185 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(6.283185 * gameTime));
	output.stage0.uv.y = s_stage0*sin(6.283185 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * cos(6.283185 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(6.283185 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(6.283185 * gameTime));
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	 float s_stage1 = output.stage1.uv.x;
	 float t_stage1 = output.stage1.uv.y;
	output.stage1.uv.x = s_stage1*cos(-2.251475 * gameTime) + t_stage1 * -sin(-2.251475 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(-2.251475 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(-2.251475 * gameTime));
	output.stage1.uv.y = s_stage1*sin(-2.251475 * gameTime) + t_stage1 * cos(-2.251475 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(-2.251475 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(-2.251475 * gameTime));

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_
	destination = (tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv)) + (destination);

	// stage1_
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/modelsmodels_weapons2_bfg_bfg_e_generated.fx
// Shader: models/weapons2/bfg/bfg_e
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_envmapbfg;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_envmapbfg;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;
// stage2's externs
uniform texture stage2_tinfx;
uniform float3x2 stage2_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_envmapbfg>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_envmapbfg>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage2_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage2_tinfx>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};
struct stage2_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD2;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
	stage2_input stage2;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 1 - sin(((((input.position.x + input.position.z) * 0.001 + (0.1 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.5;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 1 - sin(((((input.position.y) * 0.001 + (0.1 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.5;
	output.stage0.uv.x *= 2.5;
	output.stage0.uv.y *= 2.5;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 0.2 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.y += -0.2 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv.x += 1 - sin(((((input.position.x + input.position.z) * 0.001 + (0.1 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.5;
	output.stage1.uv.y += 1 - sin(((((input.position.y) * 0.001 + (0.1 * gameTime))) % 1025) * 6.283185) * 0.5;
	output.stage1.uv.x *= 5;
	output.stage1.uv.y *= 5;
	output.stage1.uv.x += 0.3 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv.y += 0.6 * gameTime;
	output.stage2.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_envmapbfg
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_envmapbfg
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv)) + (destination);

	// stage2_tinfx
	destination = (tex2D(stage2_sampler, input.stage2.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

// Shader: models/weapons2/bfg/bfg
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_tinfx2d;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_bfg;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_tinfx2d>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_bfg>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 0.01 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 0.01 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_tinfx2d
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_bfg
	float4 stage1_source = tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv);
	destination = (stage1_source * stage1_source.a) + (destination * (1.0 -stage1_source.a));

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/modelsmodels_weapons2_plasma_plasma_glo_generated.fx
// Shader: models/weapons2/plasma/plasma_glo
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_plasma_glo;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;
// stage1's externs
uniform texture stage1_tinfxb;
uniform float3x2 stage1_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_plasma_glo>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};
sampler stage1_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage1_tinfxb>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};
struct stage1_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD1;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
	stage1_input stage1;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	 float s_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.x;
	 float t_stage0 = output.stage0.uv.y;
	output.stage0.uv.x = s_stage0*cos(0.5759587 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * -sin(0.5759587 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(0.5759587 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(0.5759587 * gameTime));
	output.stage0.uv.y = s_stage0*sin(0.5759587 * gameTime) + t_stage0 * cos(0.5759587 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(0.5759587 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(0.5759587 * gameTime));
	output.stage0.uv.x += 0.7 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 1 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage1.uv.x += 0.01 * gameTime;
	output.stage1.uv.y += 0.02 * gameTime;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_plasma_glo
	destination = tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv);

	// stage1_tinfxb
	destination = (tex2D(stage1_sampler, input.stage1.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

	}

{

	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;

	output.stage1.uv = input.texcoords;
	 float s_stage1 = output.stage1.uv.x;
	 float t_stage1 = output.stage1.uv.y;
	output.stage1.uv.x = s_stage1*cos(-3.490659 * gameTime) + t_stage1 * -sin(-3.490659 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * cos(-3.490659 * gameTime)+ 0.5 *sin(-3.490659 * gameTime));
	output.stage1.uv.y = s_stage1*sin(-3.490659 * gameTime) + t_stage1 * cos(-3.490659 * gameTime) + (0.5 - 0.5 * sin(-3.490659 * gameTime)- 0.5 *cos(-3.490659 * gameTime));

// Shader: models/powerups/holdable/medkit_sphere
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_envmapdim;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_envmapdim>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_envmapdim
	destination = (tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}

// C:/Users/a.zimmer/Documents/Visual Studio 2017/Projects/Water3D/Water3D/bin/Debug/Content/q3/scripts/modelsmodels_powerups_holdable_medkit_fluid_generated.fx
// Shader: models/powerups/holdable/medkit_fluid
// Generic Externs
uniform float4x4 worldViewProj;
uniform float gameTime;
// stage0's externs
uniform texture stage0_medkit_fluid;
uniform float3x2 stage0_tcmod;

sampler stage0_sampler = sampler_state
{
	Texture = <stage0_medkit_fluid>;
	minfilter = LINEAR;
	magfilter = LINEAR;
	mipfilter = NONE;
	AddressU = Wrap;
	AddressV = Wrap;
};

struct stage0_input
{
	float2 uv : TEXCOORD0;
};

struct VertexShaderInput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	float3 normal : NORMAL0;
	float2 texcoords : TEXCOORD0;
	float2 lightmapcoords : TEXCOORD1;
	float4 diffuse : COLOR0;
};

struct VertexShaderOutput
{
	float4 position : POSITION0;
	stage0_input stage0;
};

VertexShaderOutput VertexShaderProgram(VertexShaderInput input)
{
	VertexShaderOutput output;
	output.position = mul(input.position, worldViewProj);
	output.stage0.uv = input.texcoords;
	output.stage0.uv.x += 0 * gameTime;
	output.stage0.uv.y += 2 * gameTime;

	return output;
};

float4 PixelShaderProgram(VertexShaderOutput input) : COLOR0
{
	float4 destination = (float4)0;
	float4 source = (float4)0;

	// stage0_medkit_fluid
	destination = (tex2D(stage0_sampler, input.stage0.uv)) + (destination);

	destination.a = 1.0;

	return destination;
}

technique Technique1
{
	pass Pass1
	{
		VertexShader = compile vs_4_0_level_9_1 VertexShaderProgram();
		PixelShader = compile ps_4_0_level_9_1 PixelShaderProgram();
	}
}
